visibility pack
itemRgb on
spectrum off

track problems
type bigBed 3
shortLabel _model_problems
longLabel Separate problems (PeakSegFPOP looks for multiple peaks in each region, independently for each sample)
visibility pack
itemRgb off
spectrum off
bigDataUrl http://hubs.hpc.mcgill.ca/~thocking/PeakSegFPOP-/problems.bigBed

track jointProblems
type bigBed 3
shortLabel _model_jointProblems
longLabel Joint problems (PeakSegJoint looks for one common peak in each region, across all samples)
visibility pack
itemRgb off
spectrum off
bigDataUrl http://hubs.hpc.mcgill.ca/~thocking/PeakSegFPOP-/jointProblems.bigBed

track peaks_summary
type bigBed 5
shortLabel _model_peaks_summary
longLabel Regions with a peak in at least one sample
visibility pack
itemRgb off
spectrum on
bigDataUrl http://hubs.hpc.mcgill.ca/~thocking/PeakSegFPOP-/peaks_summary.bigBed

visibility pack
itemRgb on
spectrum off

track problems
type bigBed 3
shortLabel _model_problems
longLabel Separate problems (PeakSegFPOP looks for multiple peaks in each region, independently for each sample)
visibility pack
itemRgb off
spectrum off
bigDataUrl http://hubs.hpc.mcgill.ca/~thocking/PeakSegFPOP-/problems.bigBed

track jointProblems
type bigBed 3
shortLabel _model_jointProblems
longLabel Joint problems (PeakSegJoint looks for one common peak in each region, across all samples)
visibility pack
itemRgb off
spectrum off
bigDataUrl http://hubs.hpc.mcgill.ca/~thocking/PeakSegFPOP-/jointProblems.bigBed

track peaks_summary
type bigBed 5
shortLabel _model_peaks_summary
longLabel Regions with a peak in at least one sample
visibility pack
itemRgb off
spectrum on

track problems
type bigBed 3
shortLabel _model_problems
longLabel Separate problems (PeakSegFPOP looks for multiple peaks in each region, independently for each sample)
visibility pack
itemRgb off
spectrum off

track jointProblems
type bigBed 3
shortLabel _model_jointProblems
longLabel Joint problems (PeakSegJoint looks for one common peak in each region, across all samples)
visibility pack
itemRgb off
